# cpp_codes_and_learning_project
</head><body><h1 style="padding-top: 3pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">C++ Cheat Sheet</h1><h2 style="padding-top: 22pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Syntax</h2><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Let’s kick off our C++ reference sheet with syntax.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">using namespace </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Hello World!&quot;</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">return </span><span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><ul id="l1"><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 42pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;"><b>Line 1: </b>‘#include &lt;iostream&gt;’ specifies the <i>header file library</i>, which helps you deal with input and output objects like “cout.” Header files are used to add specific functionality to C++ programs.</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 42pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Line 2: <span class="p">‘using namespace std’ allows you to use names for objects and variables from the standard library.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: justify;">Line 3: <span class="p">Blank line. C++ ignores the spaces present within the code.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 42pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Line 4: <span class="p">‘int main()’, which is a function. Any code within the curly brackets {} will be executed.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 42pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Line 5: <span class="p">cout is an object used along with the insertion operator (&lt;&lt;) to print the output text.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Line 6: <span class="p">return 0 is used to end the main function.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">While writing code in C++, always make sure you end each line with a semicolon to specify the end of the line. You must also add the closing bracket to end the main function; otherwise, you’ll get errors while compiling the code.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Comments</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">In C++, the compiler ignores the text followed by the comments. C++ supports two different types of comments:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">//: <span class="p">specifies the single-line comment.</span></p><p class="s7" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">/* ….*/<span class="p">: specifies the multi-line comment.</span></p><h2 style="padding-top: 3pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Data Types</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-bottom: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Data types specify the type of the data variable. The compiler allocates the memory based on the data types. The following are the C++ data types:</p><p style="padding-left: 8pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span><table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"><tr><td>![image](https://github.com/Yasser-Jemli/cpp_codes_and_learning_project/assets/92098387/86b19cd5-933e-49d1-b56c-2f9cab0864dc)
/></td></tr></table></span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-top: 7pt;padding-left: 42pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Built-in or primitive data types: <span class="p">Pre-defined data types that can be used directly, including Integer, Character, Boolean, Floating Point, Double Floating Point, Valueless or Void, and Wide Character.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 42pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Derived data types: <span class="p">Derived from primitive data types: function, array, pointer, and reference.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 42pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">User-defined data types: <span class="p">Defined by users: class, structure, union, enumeration, and Typedef.</span></p></li></ul><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Variables</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Variables store the data values. C++ supports various types of variables, such as int, double, string, char, and float.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-bottom: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>num = <span style=" color: #986700;">12</span>; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// Integer</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>name = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Unity Buddy&quot;</span>; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// String(text) </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">char </span>ch = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;U&#39;</span>; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">//character</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">float </span>fl = <span style=" color: #986700;">5.99</span>; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// Floating point number</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">You can use alphabets, numbers, and the underscore for a variable name. However, variables cannot start with numbers or the underscore ‘_’ character. Instead, they begin with letters</p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">followed by numbers or the underscore ‘_’ character. Moreover, you cannot use a keyword for the variable name.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Variables Scope</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">In C++, you can declare your variables within three parts of the program, also known as the scope of the variables:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h4 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Local Variables</h4><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">These variables are declared within a function or block of code. Their scope is only limited to that function or block and cannot be accessed by any other statement outside that block.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">using namespace </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s9" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">// Local variable: <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">a, b;</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #373A41;">c;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s9" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// initialization</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">a = <span style=" color: #986700;">10</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">b = <span style=" color: #986700;">20</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">c = a + b; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; c;</p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h4 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Global Variables</h4><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Global variables are accessible to any function, method, or block of the program. Usually, it is defined outside all the functions. The value of the global variable is the same throughout the program.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s10" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt;</span></p><p style="padding-left: 8pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s12" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">using namespace <span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s15" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">// Global variable: <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">g;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s12" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s15" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">// Local variable: <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">a, b;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s15" style="padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// initialization</p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">a = <span style=" color: #986700;">10</span>;</p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">b = <span style=" color: #986700;">20</span>;</p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">g = a + b;</p><p class="s14" style="padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 31pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; g; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">return </span><span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>;</p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 8pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Data Type Modifiers</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Data type modifiers are used to modify a data type’s maximum length of data. The following table will help you understand the size and range of built-in data types when combined with modifiers. There are four different types of modifiers available in C++, namely signed, unsigned, short, and long.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><table style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:7.37499pt" cellspacing="0"><tr style="height:20pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Data Type</p></td><td class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Size (in bytes)</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" colspan="2"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Range</p></td></tr><tr style="height:19pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">short int</p></td><td class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">2</p></td><td colspan="2"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">-32,768 to 32,767</p></td></tr><tr style="height:20pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">unsigned short int</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">2</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" colspan="2"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">0 to 65,535</p></td></tr><tr style="height:19pt"><td class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">unsigned int</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p colspan="2"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">0 to 4,294,967,295</p></td></tr><tr style="height:34pt"><td left;">2,147,483,647</p></td><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s18" style="padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">long int</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">-2,147,483,648</p><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">2,147,483,647</p></td><td style="width:35pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-right: 2pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: right;">to</p></td></tr><tr style="height:19pt"><td style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p></td></tr><tr style="height:20pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">wchar_t</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">2 or 4</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">1 wide character</p></td></tr></table><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Literals</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Literals in C++ are data that you can use to represent the fixed values. You can use them directly within the code.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example, 1, 2.5, “s”, etc.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">There are different types of literal available in C++, as explained below:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Integer literal</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">An integer literal is numeric and does not have any fractional or exponential part. For example:</p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Decimal (base 10): 0, -9, 22, etc.</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Octal (base 8) : 021, 077, 033, etc. Hexadecimal (base 16): 0x7f, 0x2a, 0x521, etc.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Floating-Point Literals</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">These are numeric literals that have either a fractional part or an exponent part. For example: (-2.0, 0.8589, -0.26E -5).</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Character Literal</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">These are single characters enclosed within a single quote. For example: ‘a’, ‘F’, ‘2’, etc.</p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Escape Sequences</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">You can use escape sequences in C++ for untypable characters that have special meaning in C++.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><table style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:7.37499pt" cellspacing="0"><tr style="height:34pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 3pt;padding-left: 1pt;padding-right: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Escape Sequences</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s17" style="padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Characters</p></td></tr><tr style="height:20pt"><td bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Backspace</p></td></tr><tr style="height:19pt"><td bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">\f</p></td><td bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Form feed</p></td></tr><tr style="height:19pt"><td bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">\n</p></td><td 3pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Constants</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">To create a variable for which you do not want to change the values, you can use the “const” keyword.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">const int </span>LIGHT_SPEED = <span style=" color: #986700;">2997928</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">LIGHT_SPEED = <span style=" color: #986700;">2500 </span><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// cannot change the value</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Math Functions</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: bgcolor="#E7E8EB"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Returns the hyperbolic tangent of a double value</p></td></tr></table><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">User Inputs</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">C++ supports “cout” and “cin” for displaying outputs and for taking inputs from users, respectively. The cout uses the iteration operator (&lt;&lt;), and cin uses (&gt;&gt;).</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #373A41;">x; </span><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// declaring a variable</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Type a number: &quot;</span>; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// Type any number and hit enter </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">cin </span>&gt;&gt; x; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// Get user input from the keyboard</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Your number is: &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; x; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// Display the value</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Strings</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">A string is a collection or sequence of characters enclosed within double-quotes. For example:</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>str= <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Hello&quot;</span>;</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">To use string within your code, you must include the string library using this code line:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;string&gt;</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">C++ will then allow you to perform various functions to manipulate strings. The following table describes the function names and their descriptions:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><table style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:5.87499pt" 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">C++ supports different types of operators to add logic to your code and perform operations on variables and their respective values. Here are the C++ operator types:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Arithmetic Operators</h3><p bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">For assigning a value to the variable.</p></td><td left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Comparison Operators</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">You can use these operators to compare two values to return a true or false value. It will return true if both the values match, and false if they don’t match.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><table style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:7.37499pt" cellspacing="0"><tr style="height:20pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Operator</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Name</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Example</p></td></tr><tr style="height:19pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">==</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Equal to</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">x == y</p></td></tr><tr style="height:20pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">!=</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Not equal</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">x != y</p></td></tr></table><table style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:7.37499pt" cellspacing="0"><tr style="height:19pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">&gt;</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Greater than</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">x &gt; y</p></td></tr><tr style="height:19pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">&lt;</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Less than</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">x &lt; y</p></td></tr><tr style="height:34pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">&gt;=</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Greater than or equal to</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">x &gt;= y</p></td></tr><tr style="height:34pt"><td style="width:104pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">&lt;=</p></td><td style="width:93pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;padding-right: 2pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Less than or equal to</p></td><td style="width:134pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">x &lt;= y</p></td></tr></table><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Logical Operators</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">These operators determine the logic between variables.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><table style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:7.37499pt" cellspacing="0"><tr style="height:20pt"><td style="width:59pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Operator</p></td><td style="width:69pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Name</p></td><td style="width:207pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Description</p></td><td style="width:116pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s17" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Example</p></td></tr><tr style="height:31pt"><td style="width:59pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">&amp;&amp;</p></td><td style="width:69pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Logical and</p></td><td style="width:207pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Returns true if both statements are true</p></td><td style="width:116pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">x &lt; 5 &amp;&amp; x &lt; 10</p></td></tr><tr style="height:34pt"><td style="width:59pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">||</p></td><td style="width:69pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Logical or</p></td><td style="width:207pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Returns true if one of the statements is true</p></td><td style="width:116pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">x &lt; 5 || x &lt; 4</p></td></tr><tr style="height:33pt"><td style="width:59pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">!</p></td><td style="width:69pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Logical not</p></td><td style="width:207pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Reverse the result, returns false if the result is true</p></td><td style="width:116pt;border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1pt;border-top-color:#CCCCCC;border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:1pt;border-left-color:#CCCCCC;border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1pt;border-bottom-color:#CCCCCC;border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:1pt;border-right-color:#CCCCCC" bgcolor="#F7FAFF"><p class="s18" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">!(x &lt; 5 &amp;&amp; x &lt; 10)</p></td></tr></table><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Decision-Making Statements</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Decision-making statements in C++ decide the flow of program execution. Here, programmers specify more than one condition. If a condition holds true the statements in that block are executed. Otherwise, the statements from other blocks are executed instead.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">C++ has various decision-making instructions:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><ul id="l2"><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">If statement</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">if..else statement</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Switch statement</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Nested if statement</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Nested switch statement</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Ternary operator</p></li></ul><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">If Statement</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">This is the most basic type of decision-making statement. It instructs the compiler to execute the block of code only if the condition holds true.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Syntax:</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">if <span style=" color: #373A41;">(expression)</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">{ <span class="s19">//code}</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">using namespace </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span><span style=" color: #4078F1;">main </span>() { <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>b = <span style=" color: #986700;">10</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">if</span>( b &lt; <span style=" color: #986700;">20 </span>) {</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 65pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;b is less than 20;&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;value of a is : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; b &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">If..Else Statement</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">This is an extension of the ‘if’ statement. It instructs the compiler to execute the ‘if’ block only if the specified condition is true. Otherwise, it executes the ‘else’ block.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Syntax:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">if <span style=" color: #373A41;">(expression)</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">{<span class="s19">//code} </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">else</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">{<span class="s19">//code}</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">using namespace </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span><span style=" color: #4078F1;">main </span>() { <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>b = <span style=" color: #986700;">10</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">if</span>( b &lt; <span style=" color: #986700;">20 </span>) {</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 65pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;b is less than 20;&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;value of a is : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; b &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Switch Statement</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">When you need to execute conditions against various values, you can use switch statements. Syntax:</p><p class="s3" style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 11pt;text-align: left;">switch<span style=" color: #373A41;">(expression) {</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 36pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #373A41;">constant-expression statement(s);</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 36pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">break<span style=" color: #373A41;">; </span><span class="s19">//optional</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 36pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #373A41;">constant-expression statement(s);</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 36pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">break<span style=" color: #373A41;">; </span><span class="s19">//optional</span></p><p class="s5" style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 11pt;text-align: left;">:</p><p class="s5" style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 11pt;text-align: left;">:</p><p class="s3" style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 11pt;text-align: left;">default <span style=" color: #373A41;">: </span><span class="s19">//Optional</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">statement(s);</p><p class="s5" style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 11pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">using namespace </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// local variable declaration: </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">char </span>grade = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;D&#39;</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">switch<span style=" color: #373A41;">(grade) { </span>case <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;A&#39; </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Outstanding!&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">break</span>;</p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;B&#39; </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;C&#39; </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Well done&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">break</span>;</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;D&#39; </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Pass&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">break</span>;</p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;F&#39; </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Try again&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">break</span>;</p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">default <span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Invalid grade&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Your grade is &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; grade &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Nested If Statement</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">This is an “if” statement inside another “if” statement. You can use this type of statement when you need to base a specific condition on the result of another condition.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Syntax:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">if</span>( boolean_expression <span style=" color: #986700;">1</span>) {</p><p class="s20" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Executes when the boolean expression 1 is true</p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">if</span>(boolean_expression <span style=" color: #986700;">2</span>) {</p><p class="s20" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Executes when the boolean expression 2 is true</p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">using namespace </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// local variable declaration: </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>x = <span style=" color: #986700;">100</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>y = <span style=" color: #986700;">200</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">if</span>( x == <span style=" color: #986700;">100 </span>) { <span style=" color: #A625A3;">if</span>( y == <span style=" color: #986700;">200 </span>) {</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Value of x is 100 and y is 200&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Exact value of x is : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; x &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Exact value of y is : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; y &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Nested Switch Statement</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">You can include one switch statement within another switch statement. Syntax:</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">switch<span style=" color: #373A41;">(ch1) { </span>case <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;A&#39;</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;This A is part of outer switch&quot;</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">switch</span>(ch2) {</p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;A&#39;</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 77pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;This A is part of inner switch&quot;</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">break</span>;</p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;B&#39;</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">: </span><span class="s19">// ...</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">break<span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&#39;B&#39;</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">: </span><span class="s19">// ...</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">using namespace </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span><span style=" color: #4078F1;">main </span>() { <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>x = <span style=" color: #986700;">100</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>y = <span style=" color: #986700;">200</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">switch<span style=" color: #373A41;">(x) { </span>case <span style=" color: #986700;">100</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;This is part of outer switch&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">switch</span>(y) {</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 77pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">case <span style=" color: #986700;">200</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 95pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;This is part of inner switch&quot; </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 59pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Exact value of x is : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; x &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Exact value of y is : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; y &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Ternary Operator</h3><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Exp1 ? Exp2 : Exp3;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">First, expression Exp1 is evaluated. If it’s true, then Exp2 is evaluated and becomes the value of the entire ‘?’ expression. If Exp1 is false, then Exp3 is evaluated and its value becomes the value of the expression.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Loops</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Loops are used to execute a particular set of commands for a specific number of time based on the result of the evaluated condition. C++ includes the following loops</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><ul id="l3"><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">While loop</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Do-while loop</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">For loop</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Break statement</p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Continue statement</p></li></ul><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">While Loop</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">The loop will continue till the specified condition is true.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">while <span style=" color: #373A41;">(condition)</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">{code}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Do-While Loop</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">When the condition becomes false, the do-while loop stops executing. However, the only difference between the while and do-while loop is that the do-while loop tests the condition <i>after </i>executing the loop. Therefore, the loop gets executed at least once.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">do</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">{</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Code</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">while <span style=" color: #373A41;">(condition)</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For Loop</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">You can use the for loop to execute a block of code multiple times. This loop runs the block until the condition specified in it holds false.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">for </span>(<span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>a=<span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>; i&lt; count; i++)</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">{</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Code</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Break Statement</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">This is used to break the flow of the code so the remaining code isn’t executed. This brings you out of the loop.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">for </span>(<span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>i = <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>; i &lt; <span style=" color: #986700;">10</span>; i++) { <span style=" color: #A625A3;">if </span>(i == <span style=" color: #986700;">4</span>) {</p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">break<span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; i &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;\n&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Continue Statement</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">This statement will break the flow and take you to the evaluation of the condition. Later, it starts the code execution again.</p><p style="padding-top: 3pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">for </span>(<span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>i = <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>; i &lt; <span style=" color: #986700;">10</span>; i++) { <span style=" color: #A625A3;">if </span>(i == <span style=" color: #986700;">4</span>) {</p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">continue<span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; i &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;\n&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Arrays</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Arrays are derived data types that store multiple data items of similar types at contiguous memory locations.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>vehicles [<span style=" color: #986700;">4</span>];
