<span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">//declaring array to store up to 4 variables. </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>vehicles[<span style=" color: #986700;">4</span>]= {<span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;car&quot;</span>, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;scooter&quot;</span>, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;cycle&quot;</span>, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;bike&quot;</span>}; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">//initializing the array</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Accessing Array Values</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">You need to use the index number to access the elements stored in an array.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>vehicles[<span style=" color: #986700;">4</span>]= {<span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;car&quot;</span>, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;scooter&quot;</span>, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;cycle&quot;</span>, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;bike&quot;</span>}; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; vehicles [<span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>];</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Changing Array Elements</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">You can change the elements stored in an array using the index number.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>vehicles[<span style=" color: #986700;">4</span>]= {<span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;car&quot;</span>, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;scooter&quot;</span>, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;cycle&quot;</span>, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;bike&quot;</span>}; vehicles [<span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>]= <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot; &quot;</span>airplane<span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;;</span></p><p class="s2" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">cout &lt;&lt; vehicles[0];</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><h2 style="padding-top: 3pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Functions</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">A function is a group of instructions to carry out a specific task. The common function in every C++ program is the main() function. You can even break down your complex code into multiple small functions and execute them separately.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">For this, you need to declare, define, and call that function. C++ has several built-in functions that you can call directly within any program.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Defining a Function</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">The following is the syntax for defining a function in C++:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">return_type <span style=" color: #4078F1;">function_name</span>( parameter <span style=" color: #C18300;">list </span>) { body of the function</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Where:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><ul id="l4"><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">return_type <span class="p">specifies the type of value being returned by that function.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">function_name <span class="p">specifies the name of the function and needs to be unique.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 42pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">parameter list <span class="p">allows you to pass more than one value to your function, along with their data types.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">body of the function <span class="p">specifies the set of instructions to accomplish a task.</span></p></li></ul><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s12" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: -19pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">max</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">(</span>int <span style=" color: #373A41;">num1, </span>int <span style=" color: #373A41;">num2) { </span><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// declaring the function max </span>int <span style=" color: #373A41;">result;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s12" style="padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -19pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">if <span style=" color: #373A41;">(num1 &gt; num2) result = num1;</span></p><p class="s12" style="padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">else</p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">result = num2;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s12" style="padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #373A41;">result;</span></p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Calling a Function</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">You must call a function wherever you need it in your program. For example:</p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">using namespace </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s9" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// function declaration</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">max</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">(</span>int <span style=" color: #373A41;">num1, </span>int <span style=" color: #373A41;">num2);</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 6pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>a = <span style=" color: #986700;">100</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>b = <span style=" color: #986700;">200</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>ret;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">ret = max(a, b);</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Max value is : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; ret &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Function Arguments</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">You can pass arguments in three ways:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><ul id="l5"><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 78pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Call by value: <span class="p">Passes the actual value of an argument into the formal parameter of the function. It will not make any change to the parameter inside the function and does not effect on the argument.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 78pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Call by pointer: <span class="p">You can copy an argument address into the formal parameter. Here, the address accesses the actual argument used in the call. This means that changes made to the parameter affect the argument.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 78pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Call by reference: <span class="p">You can copy an argument reference into the formal parameter. The reference accesses the actual argument used in the call. This means that changes made to the parameter affect the argument.</span></p></li></ul><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Storage Classes</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Storage classes define the visibility of the variables and functions. C++ supports various storage classes, like auto, register, extern, static, and mutable.</p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Auto Storage Class</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">By default, C++ uses this storage class for all variables. For example:</p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">{</p><p class="s12" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #373A41;">var;</span></p><p class="s12" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">auto int <span style=" color: #373A41;">var1;</span></p><p class="s14" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">You can only use the “auto” within functions for defining the local variables.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Register Storage Class</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">This storage class defines the local variables to be stored within the register rather than in RAM. It’s useful when you want to access the variable frequently, such as counters. The size of the variable will have a maximum size equal to the register size.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">{</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">register int <span style=" color: #373A41;">miles;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Static Storage Class</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">The static storage class tells the compiler to maintain local variables throughout the program without needing to create and destroy them when it comes into and goes out of scope. Defining a variable as static means it will maintain its values between function calls.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Global variables are static, which means their scope will be restricted to their declared file. If you specify a class data member as static, it creates only one copy of that member that all objects of its class will share.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// Function declaration </span>void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">func1</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">(</span>void<span style=" color: #373A41;">);</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 3pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 30pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">static int </span>count = <span style=" color: #986700;">10</span>; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">/* Global variable */ </span>main() {</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">while<span style=" color: #373A41;">(count--) { func();</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// Function definition </span>void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">func1</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">( </span>void <span style=" color: #373A41;">) {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">static int </span>i = <span style=" color: #986700;">5</span>; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// local static variable </span>i++;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span>::<span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;i is &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; i ;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span>::<span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot; and count is &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; count &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span>::<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s7" style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Extern Storage Class</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">The extern storage class provides a reference of a global variable and makes it visible to ALL the program files. When you specify a variable as ‘extern&#39;, the variable cannot be initialized because it points the variable name at a storage location that has been previously defined.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">In case of multiple files where you define a global variable or function, also to be used in other files, extern will provide a reference in another file of defined variable or function. You must use the extern modifier when you have to share the same global variables or functions between two or more files.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">count ;</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">extern void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">write_extern</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">();</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">main() {</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">count = <span style=" color: #986700;">5</span>; write_extern();</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">For example: Program 1</p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-bottom: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Program 2</p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 229%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">extern int </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">count;</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">write_extern</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">(</span>void<span style=" color: #373A41;">) {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span>::<span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Count is &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; count &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span>::<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Mutable Storage Class</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">You can use this storage class if you want an object member to override the member function. That is, a mutable member that can be modified by a const member function.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Structure</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Structure allows you to define the data items of the non-similar data types. To use a structure, you must define it and access its structure members.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">The following is the syntax for creating a structure:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span class="s21" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">struct </span><span class="s22" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">[</span><span class="s23" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">structure tag</span><span class="s22" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">] {</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span class="s24" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">  </span><span class="s22" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">member definition;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span class="s24" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">  </span><span class="s22" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">member definition;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span class="s24" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">  </span><span class="s22" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">...</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span class="s24" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">  </span><span class="s22" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">member definition;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 2pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span class="s22" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">} [one </span><span class="s21" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">or </span><span class="s22" style=" background-color: #FAFAFA;">more structure variables];</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">For example, we want to create a structure of books consisting of title, author, subject, and book_id, as follows:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">struct <span style=" color: #C18300;">Books </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">char </span>title[<span style=" color: #986700;">50</span>]; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">char </span>author[<span style=" color: #986700;">50</span>]; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">char </span>subject[<span style=" color: #986700;">100</span>]; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>book_id;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">} book;</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Accessing Structure Members</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">You must use the member access operator (.) to access structure members. This is a period between the structure variable name and the structure member that we wish to access.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-left: 12pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span>#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;cstring&gt;</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 12pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 30pt;text-align: left;">using namespace <span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">; </span>struct <span style=" color: #C18300;">Books </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 12pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">char </span>title[<span style=" color: #986700;">50</span>];</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">char </span>author[<span style=" color: #986700;">50</span>]; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">char </span>subject[<span style=" color: #986700;">100</span>]; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">int  </span>book_id;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 12pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 12pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">struct <span style=" color: #C18300;">Books Book1</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;    </span><span class="s19">// Declare Book1 of type Book</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">struct <span style=" color: #C18300;">Books Book2</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;    </span><span class="s19">// Declare Book2 of type Book</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// book 1 specification</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">strcpy</span>( Book1.title, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Learn C++ Programming&quot;</span>); <span style=" color: #C18300;">strcpy</span>( Book1.author, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Chand Miyan&quot;</span>);</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">strcpy</span>( Book1.subject, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;C++ Programming&quot;</span>); Book1.book_id = <span style=" color: #986700;">6495407</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// book 2 specification</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">strcpy</span>( Book2.title, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Telecom Billing&quot;</span>); <span style=" color: #C18300;">strcpy</span>( Book2.author, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Yakit Singha&quot;</span>); <span style=" color: #C18300;">strcpy</span>( Book2.subject, <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Telecom&quot;</span>); Book2.book_id = <span style=" color: #986700;">6495700</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Print Book1 info</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Book 1 title : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; Book1.title &lt;&lt;<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Book 1 author : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; Book1.author &lt;&lt;<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Book 1 subject : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; Book1.subject &lt;&lt;<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Book 1 id : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; Book1.book_id &lt;&lt;<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Print Book2 info</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 30pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Book 2 title : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; Book2.title &lt;&lt;<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Book 2 author : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; Book2.author &lt;&lt;<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Book 2 subject : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; Book2.subject &lt;&lt;<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Book 2 id : &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; Book2.book_id &lt;&lt;<span style=" color: #C18300;">endl</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 23pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">References</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">When you declare a variable as a reference, it acts as an alternative to the existing one. You need to specify the reference variable with “&amp;”, as shown below:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>food = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Pizza&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s4" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">string <span style=" color: #373A41;">&amp;meal = food;  </span><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// reference to food</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Pointer</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">A pointer in C++ is a variable that stores the memory address of another variable. Similar to regular variables, pointers also have data types. We use ‘*’ to declare pointers in C++.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>food = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Pizza&quot;</span>; <span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// string variable</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s4" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">cout <span style=" color: #373A41;">&lt;&lt; food; </span><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// Outputs the value of food (Pizza)</span></p><p class="s4" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">cout <span style=" color: #373A41;">&lt;&lt; &amp;food; </span><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;">// Outputs the memory address of food (0x6dfed4)</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Classes and Objects</h3><p class="s25" style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;"><a href="https://hackr.io/blog/oops-concepts-in-java-with-examples" style=" color: black; font-family:Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 11pt;" target="_blank">C++ is an </a><a href="https://hackr.io/blog/oops-concepts-in-java-with-examples" class="a" target="_blank">object-oriented </a><span style=" color: #1154CC; font-family:Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: underline; font-size: 11pt;">programming</span> <span style=" color: #000;">language with classes and objects. Class is a user-defined data type you can use to bind data members and member functions together. You can access them by creating an instance of that class.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Creating a Class</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">Here’s how to create a class in C++:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">MyClass </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{   </span><span class="s19">// The class</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:      </span><span class="s19">// Access specifier- accessible to everyone</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #373A41;">myNum;    </span><span class="s19">// Attribute (int variable)</span></p><p class="s4" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">string <span style=" color: #373A41;">myString; </span><span class="s19">// Attribute (string variable)</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Creating an Object</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Objects work as an instance of the class, allowing you to access its members, functions, and variables. You must use the dot (.) operator, as shown below:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">MyClass </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{ </span>public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #373A41;">myNum;</span></p><p class="s4" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">string <span style=" color: #373A41;">myString;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">MyClass myObj; <span class="s19">// Creating an object of MyClass</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 6pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">myObj.myNum = <span style=" color: #986700;">15</span>; myObj.myString = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Some text&quot;</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span class="s19">// Print attribute values </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; myObj.myNum &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;\n&quot;</span>; <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; myObj.myString; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">return </span><span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Creating Multiple Objects</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Here’s an example of how to create multiple objects of the same class:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">Car </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{ </span>public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s4" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">string <span style=" color: #373A41;">brand;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Create an object of Car</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Car carObj1; carObj1.brand = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;BMW&quot;</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Create another object of Car</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Car carObj2; carObj2.brand = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Ford&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Print attribute values</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; carObj1.brand <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;\n&quot;</span>;</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; carObj2.brand <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;\n&quot;</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">return </span><span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Class Methods</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Methods are like functions that are defined within a class. C++ has two types of methods: inside class and outside class.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Inside Class Method</h3><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">MyClass </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{ </span>public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">myMethod</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() { </span><span class="s19">// Method/function inside the class</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Hello World!&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">MyClass myObj;  <span class="s19">// Create an object of MyClass</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">myObj.myMethod(); <span class="s19">// Call the method</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Outside Class Method</h3><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">MyClass </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{ </span>public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">myMethod</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">(); </span><span class="s19">// Method declaration</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Method/function definition outside the class</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">void </span>MyClass::myMethod() { <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Hello World!&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">MyClass myObj;  <span class="s19">// object creation</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">myObj.myMethod(); <span class="s19">// Call the method</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Constructors</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">A constructor is a method automatically called upon object creation. It has the same name as the class name, and no data type.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 11pt;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">Fir_Class </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 12pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 35pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Fir_Class() {</p><p class="s19" style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 11pt;text-align: left;">// Constructor</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 35pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 11pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Hello World!&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 24pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 12pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Fir_Class myObj;  <span class="s19">// call the constructor</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 12pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">return <span style=" color: #986700;">0</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Access Specifiers</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Access specifiers define the access of the class members and variables. C++ supports three types of access specifiers:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><ul id="l6"><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Public: <span class="p">Class members and variables are accessible from outside the class.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 42pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Private: <span class="p">Class members and variables are accessible only within the class and not outside the class.</span></p></li><li data-list-text="●"><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 43pt;text-indent: -18pt;text-align: left;">Protected: <span class="p">Class members and variables are accessible only in their subclasses.</span></p></li></ul><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Encapsulation</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">Encapsulation helps you hide sensitive data from the users. Here, we use the private access specifier for declaring the variables and methods. If you want to allow others to read or modify those variables and methods, you must use the public get and set methods.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt;</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">using namespace <span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">Employee </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{ </span>private<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 53pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #373A41;">name;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Setter</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: -11pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">setName</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">(</span>int <span style=" color: #373A41;">n) { name= s;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Getter</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">getName</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() { </span>return <span style=" color: #373A41;">name;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() { Employee myObj;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">myObj.setName(<span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Bob&quot;</span>); <span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; myObj.getName(); <span style=" color: #A625A3;">return </span><span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Inheritance</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">C++ supports inheritance, allowing you to inherit the members and variables of one class to another. The inheriting class is the child class and the other is the parent class. You must use (:) symbol to inherit:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Parent class</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">Vehicle </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{ </span>public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>brand = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Ford&quot;</span>; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">void </span><span style=" color: #4078F1;">sound</span>() {</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;honk \n&quot; </span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Child class</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">Car</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">: </span>public <span style=" color: #373A41;">Vehicle {</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">string </span>model = <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Mustang&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() { Car myCar;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">myCar.sound();</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; myCar.brand + <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot; &quot; </span>+ myCar.model; <span style=" color: #A625A3;">return </span><span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Polymorphism</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Polymorphism specifies the “many forms.” It is the ability of a single message to be displayed in multiple forms and takes place when you have multiple child classes and one base class.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Parent class</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">Animal </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">{ </span>public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">sound</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;The animal makes a sound \n&quot; </span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Child class</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">Pig </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">: </span>public <span style=" color: #373A41;">Animal { </span>public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">sound</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;The pig says: wee wee \n&quot; </span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Derived class</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">class <span style=" color: #C18300;">Dog </span><span style=" color: #373A41;">: </span>public <span style=" color: #373A41;">Animal { </span>public<span style=" color: #373A41;">:</span></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">void <span style=" color: #4078F1;">sound</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 41pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;The dog says: bow wow \n&quot; </span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">};</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">Animal ani; Pig myPig; Dog myDog;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">ani.sound(); myPig.sound(); myDog.sound(); <span style=" color: #A625A3;">return </span><span style=" color: #986700;">0</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">File Handling</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">You can use an fstream library to handle files. The fstream library consists of &lt;iostream&gt; and</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">&lt;fstream&gt; header file.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s8" style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include &lt;iostream&gt; #include &lt;fstream&gt;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s7" style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">ofstream: <span class="p">create and write to the files. </span>ifstream: <span class="p">read from the specified file. </span>fstream: <span class="p">combination of above both.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Creating and Writing</h3><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s1" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;iostream&gt; </span>#include <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&lt;fstream&gt; </span><span style=" color: #A625A3;">using namespace </span><span style=" color: #C18300;">std</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">int <span style=" color: #4078F1;">main</span><span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Create and open a text file</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">ofstream <span style=" color: #4078F1;">MyFile</span>(<span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;filename.txt&quot;</span>);</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Write to the file</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">MyFile &lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;content&quot;</span>;</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Close the file</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">MyFile.close();</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Reading</h3><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// text string to output the text file</p><p class="s4" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">string <span style=" color: #373A41;">myText;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Read from the text file</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">ifstream <span style=" color: #4078F1;">MyReadFile</span>(<span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;filename.txt&quot;</span>);</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// for reading the file line by line</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">while <span style=" color: #373A41;">(getline (MyReadFile, myText)) {</span></p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Output the text from the file</p><p class="s4" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">cout <span style=" color: #373A41;">&lt;&lt; myText;</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s19" style="padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Close the file</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">MyReadFile.close();</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Exceptions</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">While compiling and running, you might run into errors. C++ allows you to handle and catch these errors using exception handling. The following is the syntax for exception handling that includes a try-catch block:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">try <span style=" color: #373A41;">{</span></p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Block of code to try</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">throw <span style=" color: #373A41;">exception; </span><span class="s19">// Throw an exception when a problem arise</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">catch <span style=" color: #373A41;">() {</span></p><p class="s19" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// Block of code to handle errors</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">For example:</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">try <span style=" color: #373A41;">{</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">int </span>age = <span style=" color: #986700;">10</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3;">if </span>(age &gt;= <span style=" color: #986700;">20</span>) {</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;you are old enough.&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 29pt;text-indent: -12pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">} <span style=" color: #A625A3;">else </span>{ <span style=" color: #A625A3;">throw </span><span style=" color: #986700;">505</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p class="s3" style="padding-top: 5pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">catch <span style=" color: #373A41;">(</span>int <span style=" color: #373A41;">num) {</span></p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Access denied \n&quot;</span>;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 17pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300;">cout </span>&lt;&lt; <span style=" color: #4FA14E;">&quot;Error number: &quot; </span>&lt;&lt; num;</p><p class="s5" style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 5pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">}</p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h2 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Preprocessor</h2><p style="padding-top: 8pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">The following are some in-built preprocessors available in C++ for various functionalities.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;    // Insert standard header file #include &quot;myfile.h&quot;    // Insert file in current directory #define X some text    // Replace X with some text #define F(a,b) a+b    // Replace F(1,2) with 1+2 #define X \</p><p style="padding-left: 10pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">some text      // Multiline definition</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">#undef X       // Remove definition</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">#if defined(X)     // Conditional compilation (#ifdef X) #else        // Optional (#ifndef X or #if !defined(X))</p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">#endif       // Required after #if, #ifdef</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Dynamic Memory Management</h3><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #4078F1; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">#include </span><span style=" color: #4FA14E; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;memory&gt;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">shared_ptr</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;</span><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">int</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&gt; x;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #4FA14E; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Include memory (std namespace)</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Empty shared_ptr to a integer on heap. Uses</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">reference counting for cleaning up objects.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">x = make_shared&lt;</span><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">int</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&gt;(</span><span style=" color: #986700; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">12</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">);</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">shared_ptr</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;</span><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">int</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&gt; y = x;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">2.</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">cout </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;&lt; *y;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 21pt;text-indent: -22pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">if </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">(y.get() == x.get()) { </span><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">cout </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;&lt; </span><span style=" color: #4FA14E; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&quot;Same&quot;</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">}</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">y.reset();</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 21pt;text-indent: -22pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">if </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">(y.get() != x.get()) { </span><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">cout </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;&lt; </span><span style=" color: #4FA14E; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&quot;Different&quot;</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">}</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 21pt;text-indent: -22pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">if </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">(y == </span><span style=" color: #0083BA; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">nullptr</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">) { </span><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">cout </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;&lt; </span><span style=" color: #4FA14E; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&quot;Empty&quot;</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">}</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">y = make_shared&lt;</span><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">int</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&gt;(</span><span style=" color: #986700; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">15</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">); </span><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">cout </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;&lt; *y;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">cout </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;&lt; *x; weak_ptr&lt;</span><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">int</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&gt; w;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">w = y;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6;
