font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Allocate value 12 on heap</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Copy shared_ptr, implicit changes reference count to</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Dereference y to print &#39;12&#39;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Raw pointers (here x == y)</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Eliminate one owner of object</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-top: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Can compare against nullptr (here returns true)</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Assign new value</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Dereference x to print &#39;15&#39;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Dereference x to print &#39;12&#39;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Create empty weak pointer</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// w has weak reference to y.</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">if </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">(</span><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">shared_ptr</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;</span><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">int</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&gt; s = w.lock()) { </span><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Has to be copied into a shared_ptr before</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">usage</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 21pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">cout </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;&lt; *s;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">}</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">unique_ptr</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;</span><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">int</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&gt; z;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">unique_ptr</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;</span><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">int</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&gt; q;</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">z = make_unique&lt;</span><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">int</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&gt;(</span><span style=" color: #986700; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">16</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">);</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">allowed.</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">q = move(z);</span></p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 21pt;text-indent: -22pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A625A3; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">if </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">(z == </span><span style=" color: #0083BA; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">nullptr</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">){ </span><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">cout </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;&lt; </span><span style=" color: #4FA14E; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&quot;Z null&quot;</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">}</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 14pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">cout </span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;&lt; *q; </span><span style=" color: #C18300; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">shared_ptr</span><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">&lt;B&gt; r;</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Create empty unique pointers</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Allocate int (16) on heap. Only one reference</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Move reference from z to q.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 10pt;text-align: left;"><span style=" color: #373A41; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">r = dynamic_pointer_cast&lt;B&gt;(t); </span><span style=" color: #A0A1A6; font-family:Consolas, monospace; font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-size: 10pt;">// Converts t to a shared_ptr&lt;B&gt;</span></p><p style="padding-left: 7pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"/><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-top: 4pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">Floating Point Math</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">You must include the “cmath” library to perform tasks on floating-point numbers.</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">#include &lt;cmath&gt;    // Include cmath (std namespace)</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">sin(x); cos(x); tan(x);  // you can perform Trig functions, x (double) is in radians asin(x); acos(x); atan(x); // Inverses</p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">atan2(y, x);     // atan(y/x)</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">sinh(x); cosh(x); tanh(x); // Hyperbolic sin, cos, tan functions exp(x); log(x); log10(x); // e to the x, log base e, log base 10 pow(x, y); sqrt(x);   // x to the y, square root</p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: justify;">ceil(x); floor(x);    // Round up or down (as a double) fabs(x); fmod(x, y);   // Absolute value, x mod y</p><p style="text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;"><br/></p><h3 style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: justify;">iostream.h and iostream</h3><p style="padding-top: 6pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">#include &lt;iostream&gt;   // Include iostream (std namespace)</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">cin &gt;&gt; x &gt;&gt; y;     // Read words x and y (any type) from standard input cout &lt;&lt; &quot;x=&quot; &lt;&lt; 3 &lt;&lt; endl; // Write line to stdout</p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">cerr &lt;&lt; x &lt;&lt; y &lt;&lt; flush;  // Write to stderr and flush c = cin.get();     // c = getchar();</p><p style="padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">cin.get(c);      // Read char</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">cin.getline(s, n, &#39;\n&#39;);  // Read line into char s[n] to &#39;\n&#39; (default) if (cin)       // Good state (not EOF)?</p><p style="padding-left: 92pt;text-indent: 0pt;text-align: left;">// To read/write any type T:</p><p style="padding-top: 1pt;padding-left: 6pt;text-indent: 0pt;line-height: 114%;text-align: left;">istream&amp; operator&gt;&gt;(istream&amp; i, T&amp; x) {i &gt;&gt; ...; x=...; return i;} ostream&amp; operator&lt;&lt;(ostream&amp; o, const T&amp; x) {return o &lt;&lt; ...;}</p></body></html>
